  189. In my experience this works. I've tried Realm (a different pheromone cologne, about $70 for 1.7oz back in the day) twice before with zero noticeable effect, whereas PherX has produced some definite- and interesting- results, not all of them necessarily welcome (ever been &#34;huffed&#34; by a teenager? It's a little awkward). I've been using PherX on and off for over two years now, and I've experimented with it enough that I can say with confidence that it works for me.<br /><br />I originally bought this to see what effect it might have on my wife... it definitely makes her more frisky (and no, I haven't told her about it), but funnily enough she also doesn't like the PherX scent. I use another cologne on top of it (Farenheit, her favorite- and yes, her reaction is different than if I use Farenheit alone) to help with that.<br /><br />As for the mixed reviews... scent is one of the most subjective things out there. Any given cologne is going to smell differently on various people, and be received differently depending on the smeller's preferences. Pheromones may work similarly- PherX may work great for me but not so much for another, and the effect seems to vary a little depending on who's doing the smelling. Is it worth it to try it out? Without a doubt, yes. Keep in mind though, this stuff isn't a miracle brain-override. If you're a jerk or haven't showered in a week, don't expect pheromones (or anything else, really) to override that. In my experience this stuff simply makes others view you more favorably (and if they already like you, it seems to intensify that)... sometimes, though, that's all it takes to move things from &#34;friendly&#34; to &#34;interested&#34;. Point is, your mileage can and will vary, but in my opinion it's worth seeing what that mileage will be.<br /><br />I can also say that younger people seem to respond more strongly to it (or maybe they're simply more impulsive and less reserved with their reactions?). I'm 40 and happily married so that's not really a plus for me, but for the younger guys out there it may be useful.<br /><br />Last tip: DON'T spray this on your shirt or clothes. This or any other cologne, really. You want to target your the center of your bare chest, your wrists and the sides of your neck. One or two sprays on the chest, one on the wrists and rub together, then apply the excess cologne from your wrists onto the sides of your neck. Apply a little while before you go out to let it &#34;soak in&#34; and dissipate somewhat.
